<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezweren.html>bezweren</a> (32036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besweren</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bisweran</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zweren.html>zweren</a></i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bezweren.html>bezweren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:transitive.html>transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:control.html>control</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:subdue.html>subdue</a></li>

***biceps.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:biceps.html>biceps</a> (31364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:biceps.html>biceps</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two-headed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a> (1280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:bier.html>bier</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*beuzą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰews-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dross</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bigwig.html>bigwig</a> (39785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> arose <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 1730s, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:big.html>big</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wig.html>wig</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:formerly.html>Formerly</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:authority.html>authority</a> wore wigs. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bigwig.html>Bigwig</a></i> plays <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:idea.html>idea</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:authority.html>authority</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> denoted <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> larger <a href = vnd.unilang:wig.html>wig</a>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bigwig.html>bigwig</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bigwigs</b>)
